window.onerror = function onErrorFunc(msg, url, line, colno, error) {
if(!window.ta || !ta.has('ta.js_error_array.processed')) {
if(typeof js_error_array == 'undefined') {
js_error_array = [];
}
var err = error;
js_error_array[js_error_array.length] = {'msg': msg, 'error_script': url, 'line': line, 'column': colno, 'error': err, 'ready_state': document.readyState};
return true;
}
else {
if(window.ta && ta.util && ta.util.error && ta.util.error.record) {
ta.util.error.record(error, 'error post load:: ' + msg, null, {'error_script': url, 'line': line, 'column': colno, 'ready_state': document.readyState});
}
}
};
</script>

           <div class="modules-membercenter-about-me " data-ox-name="modules.membercenter.AboutMe" data-ox-context="MemberCenter_ProfileData, Errors, Member"> 
            <div class="aboutMe profileBox">
             <span class="header">About Me</span> 
             <div class="info">
              <p>Since Nov 2007</p>
              <p>Lives in Settle, United Kingdom</p>
              <p> 65+ year old male </p>
              <p>First went to Nepal in 1989, and fell in love with the place and the people. I have now visited 12 times , a couple of serious expeditions (6000 metres +) with groups of friends, and 8 treks, all with friends/family. The trips have been mainly to the mainstream trekking areas - Khumbu, Annapurna Sanctuary, Annapurna Circuit, Langtang, Rolwaling, and have included episodes of rafting, Chitwan, and generally soaking up the culture. I am fascinated by the country, and am happy to share the experience. I hope that I may help others to get as much as possible from their visit, whilst emphasising respect for the people, culture, and environment. I am now happily retired, and travelling both within the UK and to Europe with my wife, to the Alps with friends to climb and walk, to New Zealand (to visit our daughter who lives in Wellington), to Ireland to see our son, daughter-in-law, and grandsons, and to Nepal </p>
             </div>
            </div> 
           </div>
